Current Commentary

Where is the Path to Fisheries Revival? 17

— Liu

It is heard that this year's spring fishing season has been greatly reduced due to the impact of climate, and the market has been sluggish, and sales have declined. The livelihood of fishermen has been doubled. The authorities are closely carrying out strict measures to prevent piracy in the fishing industry and are thinking about improving production and sales. Although there are still many plans in the works, since the development of fisheries and the improvement of the lives of fishermen are the goals, they will surely be realized one by one.

The difficulties encountered by China's fishing industry, those from external sources, are the Japanese invasion of fishing, taking advantage of their new equipment and powerful support to compete with our fishermen in the ocean, and selling at low prices in our country. The current tax rate has greatly reduced the import tariffs on seafood, making seafood imports smooth and affecting the domestic fishing industry. Those that are internal are that fishermen adhere to old habits and often lack both capital and materials. They cannot adopt new equipment, and the country's laws and regulations are becoming stricter, and various restrictions sometimes increase the shackles of fishermen. Recently, it was reported that the fisheries of 12 counties, including Weixian and Changli in Shandong, have been greatly reduced due to the invasion of Japanese ships and the shortage of fish and salt. Shandong needs more than one million dan of fish and salt annually, but the transportation department stipulates that only 420,000 dan are released, which is less than half of the demand. Salt is a preservative for fish, and fishing boats and salt cannot be separated. There have never been strict restrictions on fishing boats carrying salt. Therefore, even if ordinary fishermen do not catch much when they go to sea, they can use the surplus salt to make up for it. If they need to buy salt, fishermen already have small expenses, and if the salt quota is restricted, fishermen will lose their support and dare not go to sea rashly. This phenomenon is not only true for the coastal fisheries of Shandong, but also for the fisheries of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The restriction of fish and salt is to prevent private sales, but if the crackdown is too strict, fishermen will feel inconvenience. For example, in recent years, fishing boats must obtain licenses before going to sea, and those without licenses will be punished. However, ordinary fishermen often do not understand the licensing procedures and go back and forth, resulting in the loss of fishing opportunities. Judging from the fishermen's own ability, they are too weak to compete with others and have been eliminated. If the country does not fully protect them and provide fishermen with convenience, China's fishing industry may not be able to stand without the invasion of external forces.

As for sales, the equipment for transportation and the methods of promotion are far behind those of foreigners. Even in Shanghai, the fish market under planning has not been realized for a long time. Shanghai's fish market has a long history, with dozens of fish shops. Before the fishing season, fishermen often borrow fishing capital from fish shops in advance. After getting fish, they use it to compensate the fish shops. At most, the amount is as high as one or two million yuan. If the fish market is established, what will be the method for the fishermen to borrow fishing capital in advance? How will the fish shops recover the fishing capital they have released? This is also a big problem. Furthermore, what will be the status of fish shops after the fish market is established? What will be their relationship with fishermen in the future? This must also be resolved first. I believe that the crisis in China's fishing industry is deepening, and the relief plan cannot be delayed. However, legislation should be precise but not harsh, and reforms should be gradual rather than too rushed. Facts should be combined with theory, and the initial stage should not be blamed for its perfection, but should seek a way for innovation. This is what I hope that all parties related to the fishing industry will think deeply, cooperate fully, and build our new fishing industry.

Silver Price Soars: Our Country Suffers Direct Impact. Minister Shi Zhaoji Visited Hull Yesterday, Expressing Concern Over U.S. Silver Policy. U.S. Treasury Secretary Indicates Continued Silver Purchases. 18

(Washington) Chinese Minister Shi Zhaoji informally explained to Secretary of State Hull today the Chinese government's concern regarding the U.S. silver policy. Subsequently, Shi issued a statement to the press, stating that China is currently facing an economic crisis, similar to the situation in the United States in 1933. However, China does not possess the same resources to resolve these difficulties. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau announced that the government will declare today that it will no longer raise the price of silver purchases. However, he also indicated that the United States will continue to purchase silver until the silver price rises to $1.29 per ounce, or until the silver reserves of the Treasury Department reach one-third of the value of its gold reserves. As for whether a new price will appear tomorrow, the Treasury Secretary declined to comment, but stated that the Treasury Department is doing its best to act according to the orders of Congress. China today reiterated to the State Department that it is deeply concerned about the soaring silver prices. (Guomin dispatch, 25th)

Manic Atmosphere in U.S. Silver Market

The silver market today presented a manic atmosphere rarely seen. Silver bloc members in Congress generally believe that the Treasury Department's silver purchase price will increase again in a few days. With the United States determined to continue purchasing silver until the price reaches $1.29, it remains questionable whether the Treasury Department can purchase a large quantity of silver on the world market. This is because speculators holding silver are greedy for huge profits and may not be willing to release it for the time being. They will probably be willing to sell only when the price is close to $1.29. If the movement to re-establish silver prices according to the same ratio as gold is to be prevented from taking effect, and the statutory silver price is not increased to $2.18, then the Treasury Department will inevitably absorb sufficient silver in order to maintain the current price of $0.7757. Senator Wheeler stated that the silver price is now only trending toward $1.29. What he wants to see is a fixed price ratio between silver and gold. He will continue to fight for the establishment of silver coinage at a ratio of 16 to 1 of gold and silver. In other words, based on the current price of gold at $35 per ounce, the price of silver would be $2.18 per ounce. Senator King stated that he wants to use silver to supplement gold, not to replace gold. The United States will be the first to adopt bimetallism, advocating it to all countries. (Reuters dispatch, 25th) Today, the New York silver price was officially set by Handy & Harman at $0.77 per ounce. This is the highest price in more than a decade. However, it is rumored that there are bidders outside the market offering $0.7725. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Joy of Silver Bloc Members in Congress

(Washington) Observers here say that if the Treasury Department implements the Silver Purchase Act of 1934, it will still need to purchase more than 1 billion ounces of silver. Silver bloc members in Congress are very happy about the recent developments and predict that within a year, they will be able to restore silver as the American monetary standard at a ratio of 16 to 1 of gold and silver. Democratic Senator Wheeler even stated that there is currently a shortage of silver, and the silver price will definitely rise above $1.29. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Mexico Prepares to Reset Currency Value

(Washington) China is not the only country directly affected by the U.S. silver purchase policy. International experts here predict that Mexico may soon also protect its silver coins to prevent them from being melted down and sold as silver bars. These experts also say that if the silver price reaches above $0.72 per ounce, it will be profitable to melt them down, taking into account transportation and insurance costs. For Indian rupees, the silver price would have to reach $1 per ounce before melting becomes profitable. Former Mexican Foreign Minister, now Ambassador to Argentina, Casasús, said in New York that he expects the silver price to rise to $1 between June and July. However, he said that the current increase in silver prices by the United States could stimulate Mexico's prosperity. Based on the current silver price, the value of the silver content in Mexican silver coins is close to the face value of the coins, so the Mexican currency will soon have to be revalued. The Mexican Finance Minister has long been prepared for this. The value of the Mexican currency will probably also be increased to match the silver price. As for the argument that Mexico's foreign trade may suffer after the currency is revalued, Casasús does not believe it. (Guomin dispatch, 25th)

(New York) Financial figures here stated that the rise in silver prices is most beneficial to foreign speculators. Private holders of silver coins may melt the coins and sell the silver for profit. In addition, the Mexican government may follow China and protest the American silver policy. Recently, the Mexican government raised the value of the Mexican peso from 3.60 pesos to the dollar to 3.5925 pesos. If the silver price continues to rise, Mexico will raise the currency value again, which it fears may harm trade with the United States, and it is therefore quite hesitant. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

American Newspaper Criticizes Silver Policy

(New York) The New York Commercial writes today, criticizing the U.S. government's silver policy, saying that this farcical silver purchase program is now entering a more acute and harmful stage. It went on to mention the speculative fever in the world market caused by the Treasury Department's increase in silver prices, saying that unscrupulous elements have now launched a campaign to raise market prices to the target of $1.29. This silver program will have a great impact on the corruption of discipline in American political life. The silver bloc members, citing the interests of a very small number of silver mines, imposed such an absurd monetary plan on the government. This kind of power gives people a practical lesson and encourages others with special relationships to disregard the cost to their own country and other countries, and legally imitate it in order to seek the same treatment. The overseas impact of the silver program is even more noteworthy. China and Mexico will certainly feel great difficulties, and India will also be affected. If the silver price rises above $1.05 per ounce, Indian rupees will be privately destroyed. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

(London) The London Financial Times criticizes Roosevelt's policy of raising silver prices, saying that the American silver purchase policy seems to be a perverse means of politicians, causing China to fall into a serious monetary contraction crisis. The newspaper represents the views of the majority of British financiers. (Guomin News Agency dispatch, 26th)

London Silver Stocks Rise

(London) Silver mining stock prices here rose today. The Financial News stated that many silver mines produce minerals that are a mixture of silver, zinc, and lead. If silver production increases, the production of zinc and lead will also inevitably increase, which may lead to overproduction and lower prices. However, the rise in silver mining stock prices did not take this into account. Only when silver prices are permanently high can large profits be made. All London newspapers regard silver as important news. The comments of financial writers all believe that President Roosevelt's true intentions are still impossible to grasp. The speed of American silver purchases is also of particular concern. Some say that the United States already has a lot of gold reserves, and they want to accumulate silver. What kind of benefit is there? If it is intended to appease silver bloc members in Congress, there are other less costly methods. The Morning Post stated that China's efforts to prevent the outflow of silver have been partially successful, but as silver prices continue to rise, smuggling will become more rampant, and China may not be able to stop it. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Toronto: Canadian silver mining stocks rose sharply. Yesterday's trading volume reached 1,847,138 shares, the highest since August of last year. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Bombay Market Suspends Trading

Bombay: The Bombay silver market temporarily suspended new trading today, fearing that soaring silver prices would cause turmoil. Brokers are now focusing on clearing old transactions. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Japan Also Raises Silver Price

(Tokyo) The Eiyo Association announced today a revised silver price of 83 yen, 87 sen, and 8 rin, an increase of 4 yen, 85 sen, and 5 rin, due to the soaring world silver prices. The daily selling price in the Tokyo silver market rose 1 sen and 8 rin from yesterday, totaling 3 sen and 2 rin and 8 rin. The buying price rose 1 sen, totaling 2 sen and 9 rin, reaching the highest price since the war. It is only a matter of time before it breaks through the selling price of 3 sen and 3 rin in January of the ninth year of the Taisho era (1920). (Dentsu dispatch, 26th)

Worldwide Silver Production Statistics

(New York) The Metal Statistics Bureau announced today that worldwide silver production in March was 15,940,000 ounces, compared to 14,869,000 ounces in January. U.S. silver production was 2,940,000 ounces, compared to 3,411,000 ounces in February. Canadian silver production was 966,000 ounces, compared to 905,000 ounces. Mexican silver production was 6,500,000 ounces, compared to 5,500,000 ounces. (Guomin dispatch, 25th)

Japan Takes a Further Step in Annexing Manchuria; Implements Economic Control; Contents of the Draft Japan-Manchukuo Treaty. 21

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of concluding a treaty between Japan and Manchukuo on the establishment of a Japan-Manchukuo Economic Commission, the two countries are simultaneously continuing to investigate and deliberate. The draft treaty has been transferred by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Office for Manchukuo Affairs. The Office will soon convene a conference of relevant officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of the Army, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs to discuss the matter. The draft prepared by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is outlined as follows: (1) The governments of Japan and Manchukuo agree to establish an economic committee in Changchun. (2) The two governments agree to consult the committee on matters concerning the Japan-Manchukuo economy in Manchukuo and the Kwantung Leased Territory. (3) The committee shall be composed of members appointed by the two governments. The chairman of the committee shall be the presiding member appointed by the Japanese government. (4) Matters before the committee shall be decided by a majority vote. (5) The two governments shall take practical measures on the decisions adopted by the committee. In order to entrust matters relating to the committee, a Japan-Manchukuo Economic Commission office shall be established at the location of the committee, with a director and staff members. In addition, the committee shall consist of three members appointed by each of the two governments. (Dentsu dispatch, 26th)

Japanese Cabinet Deliberation Council Case; Privy Council Committee Begins Review. 22

(Tokyo) The Privy Council Review Committee on the Cabinet Deliberation Council's official system met yesterday afternoon. The Privy Council side questioned the following points on the committee seat: (1) Is the Deliberation Council suspected of building a house on top of a house in the Cabinet? (2) As a result of shifting the political focus to the Cabinet Deliberation Council, is the Cabinet not a simple implementation agency? (3) What is the relationship between the scope of deliberations of the Deliberation Council and national defense and diplomacy? (4) Is it true that the Deliberation Council is intended to strengthen the Cabinet, and are party representatives serving as committee members? (5) What is the personnel policy for the committee members and the director of the Investigation Bureau, etc.? Prime Minister Okada answered all of these questions. It was decided to reopen the meeting this afternoon for continued questioning. It is expected to be completed today. As a result, the Privy Council will pass the original proposal with an ancillary resolution. (Dentsu dispatch, 26th)

(Tokyo) The Privy Council held a review meeting yesterday to deliberate on the Cabinet Investigation Bureau system. The meeting will continue today to pass the original plan and will be submitted to the general meeting on May 7. A total of 15 members will be appointed to the Investigation Bureau. British Poultry Association Intentionally Rejects Chinese Eggs; Laboratory Results Indicate They Are Unhygienic; Unfavorable Resolutions Will Be Made at Tuesday's Meeting. 23

(London) The Daily Herald reports that the British Poultry Association is scheduled to meet on Tuesday in Sevenoaks, Kent. At that time, there will be an astonishing revelation regarding the import of 700 million frozen Chinese eggs into the United Kingdom. It is said that the production conditions of Chinese eggs are extremely dirty. Samples have been subjected to fair testing by well-known chemists. The results are shocking. On one occasion, as many as 1.5 million living bacteria were found per square millimeter. The Association will prepare a special report based on the test results. The Poultry Science and Breeding Association will also propose a draft resolution at the meeting on Tuesday, pointing out that the import of Chinese eggs into the United Kingdom is a threat to public health. Murphy later stated his feelings, saying that the Philippine issue has been fully clarified, and all ministers are interested. Regarding Philippine affairs, concrete policies have been agreed upon. Washington has a friendly attitude towards the Philippine issue and expresses concern. The President and ministers have more research than before. The President's attitude is indeed that of a statesman, who can best take into account the welfare of the Filipinos and their government. German Aircraft Cross Border to Reconnoiter Fortresses; French Aircraft Patrol Northeast Border; Britain and Germany Resume Pre-War Practice of Exchanging Military Officers for Training; American Experts Disclose that Germany Has Secretly Fortified the Rhineland. 27

(Paris) German aircraft have repeatedly flown over French border fortresses four times. The French government's aviation department issued a warning today, saying that if foreign aircraft of this kind are seen again in the future, fighter planes will be dispatched to intercept them. It is also heard that the first step in France's air defense plan is to use anti-aircraft artillery to fire aerial shells, and the second step is to send military aircraft to take off and drive away foreign aircraft. However, French aircraft are ordered not to pursue them into foreign airspace. This French warning has been widely publicized, causing foreign countries to know about it and no longer violate the restricted area. (Guomin dispatch, 26th)

(Paris) The aviation department issued an order today for aircraft to patrol the area along the northeastern border of France. According to official sources, the government took this action because foreign aircraft have recently invaded restricted areas many times. It was heard that at the end of last week, a German aircraft flew over the border, proceeded to the town of Thionville, flew around the Abashu Air Station, and then flew over the new defense zone in Cattenom. Another aircraft, apparently from Saarbrücken, flew over the Wallerfangen defensive works. Such things have been seen frequently recently. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

(Berlin) Germany will quickly complete its plan to conscript 600,000 people, as its response to the League of Nations' condemnation. This point was expressed by official sources today, and Hitler is prepared to announce the defense law he had foreshadowed on March 16, implementing conscription. Germany's protest sent to the League of Nations is worded peacefully, but some leaders still advocate a stern response. If it is not issued in a government declaration, it should be reflected in practice. Therefore, the new national defense will probably be Germany's response. It is learned that the first level of conscription will report on October 1. The remaining levels will also be rapidly gathered until the number of armed personnel reaches more than 500,000. All the countries attending the League of Nations Executive Council have received Germany's brief protest and have been notified of Germany's statement of receipt. People generally expect that when Hitler announces the new national defense law, he will also reaffirm to the world that Germany is seeking peace. The German government is also prepared to participate in any conference to maintain European peace, as long as Germany's position is absolutely equal to that of other countries. It is learned that Britain and Germany have resumed the pre-war practice of exchanging army officers to study each other's military plans and strategies. The two countries have each sent one infantry, cavalry, and artillery officer to receive six weeks of training. According to unofficial sources, Germany also made the same proposal to Japan, saying that if Japan agrees, it may be possible to exchange more officers, and the study period may also be longer. Paris is not surprised by the accelerated progress of German armaments. French officials said that they had anticipated this, so France is also proceeding with its original plan to encircle Germany. The French-Russian military agreement has already been agreed upon by both parties and can be signed next week. It is also learned that Foreign Minister Laval is scheduled to go to Moscow on May 6 to complete the final procedures of the agreement and discuss the proposed Russian-Czech agreement with Russian officials. (Guomin dispatch, 26th)

(London) Regarding Germany's reorganization of its air force, the Daily Express recently disclosed startling news, saying, "The first-line aircraft possessed by Germany to defend its mainland is more than twice that of Britain. When British and German cabinet members were talking in Berlin, German leader Hitler told British Foreign Secretary Simon that the German air force has reached an equal position with Britain. The so-called equality does not refer to the 400 aircraft possessed by Britain in the mainland, but includes the 1,020 first-line aircraft possessed by the British Royal Air Force in the entire empire." (Havas dispatch, 16th)

(New York) Simms, an American expert on foreign affairs, recently disclosed in an article in the World News, saying that although the left bank of the Rhine River is prohibited from installing armaments by the Treaty of Versailles, Germany is still actively fortifying the area and storing a large number of military supplies there. The Rhineland National Socialist Army has secretly been reorganized into regular troops. Between the Rhine River and the Meuse River, there are several battalions of engineers who use the excuse of dredging the river, but in fact, they are building large-scale defensive structures. From the city of Cologne to the Swiss border, concrete and steel cellars and heavy artillery mounting sites are being built everywhere. The police stationed on the left bank of the Rhine River number 60,000, who can be immediately converted into troops. In addition, there are 36,000 elite soldiers who are temporarily training in camps. Military figures claim that once the soldiers training in the camps in the Rhineland are formed into formal divisions, Hitler can immediately declare this fait accompli. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Tokyo) According to military sources, Japan is very happy to discuss an agreement with Germany to exchange military officers to study each other's military strategies. This kind of informal exchange has been going on for several years. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Germany States That it Still Wishes to Continue Negotiations, Takes a Cautious Attitude Towards MacDonald's Remarks 29

(Berlin) German newspapers are generally taking a cautious attitude towards British Prime Minister MacDonald's advice to Germany. It is believed that all newspapers are awaiting instructions from the authorities before offering criticism. Diplomatic circles believe that "Germany has temporarily suspended its thinking." Judging from the tone of the newspapers and government spokespersons, Germany does not want to close the door to negotiations. Many of Hitler's advisors value maintaining friendly relations with Britain. Since British Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Berlin, Germany has been paying attention to the Soviet Union's welcome of British Lord Privy Seal Eden, the united front taken by Britain, France, and Italy at the Stresa Conference, and the actions of its major ally Poland in voting against Germany in Geneva. It is widely believed that Germany has now suspended considering the impact of its policies on neighboring countries. (Reuters, 26th)

(Paris) After British Prime Minister MacDonald published an article in the National Labour Party's official newspaper, the *News Communication Magazine*, criticizing Germany, all newspapers here, because of the unusual qualifications of the author, expressed surprise on the one hand and satisfaction on the other, seeing in it the clarity of the British national character. *Le Figaro* stated that MacDonald, as the head of government and usually treating Germany with sincerity, has now issued such a discussion, then the great mistakes made by the German authorities can be estimated. Furthermore, the attitude that Germany can express towards the Stresa Conference and the League of Nations Administrative Council is purely artificial and lacks sincerity, which has been revealed by MacDonald's words. "MacDonald then warned Germany that Britain's position is consistent with that of France and Italy, which in Britain is a conscious and carefully considered one." *L'Ordre* said, "Although this belief of Prime Minister MacDonald is not something that can be established overnight, since such a belief has arisen, he does not hesitate to express it clearly, which will shock the British people, and most Britons will wait and see what the German authorities do, so as not to be deceived." (Havas, 26th)

(London) After Prime Minister MacDonald published an article in the National Labour Party's official newspaper, the *News Communication Magazine*, criticizing Germany, the Liberal Party and Labour Party opposition newspapers expressed dissatisfaction with the Prime Minister's arguments, hoping that Germany could eventually join the collective security system. The *Daily Herald* stated that the Prime Minister's article was harmful and unhelpful, and it was a pity that it could cause debate outside the League of Nations. The *News Chronicle* stated that it was inappropriate for the Prime Minister to formally express his views at this critical juncture in the peace negotiations. *The Times* reported on MacDonald's article without commenting on it. The Conservative Party's *Daily Telegraph* stated that the Prime Minister's open and honest move was to be congratulated. This kind of argument, coming from the mouth of a British Prime Minister who is deeply fond of peace, is sufficient to represent the true psychology of the governments of European countries. From a comparison of the air force strength of Britain and Germany, we know that the Prime Minister's words are not wrong. (Havas, 26th)

Germany Restricts Newspaper Operators, Prohibits Non-Aryans from Publishing Newspapers 33

(Berlin) In the future, German newspapers can only be published by individuals, groups, or organizations permitted by Amann, the de facto dictator of German publications and master of information for the National Socialist Party. This was stipulated in the new law announced tonight. The most important provision is to prohibit joint-stock companies, public organizations, professional groups, cooperative groups, and similar organizations or non-Aryans from publishing newspapers. It also stipulates that publishers must clarify that all those who have financial relationships with the newspaper and their spouses are of Aryan descent, and must go back to the year 1800. There is a six-month grace period to comply with the law. It is widely believed that several of the oldest non-partisan newspapers and Catholic newspapers, if they do not receive approval for leniency, will not be able to survive. Amann has the inherent right to issue this. (Reuters, 26th)

(Berlin) German Interior Minister Frick has recently issued an order that, in the future, the party flag and the national flag of Germany should prioritize the party flag. Although government offices and public buildings will continue to display the party and national flags side by side, when there is only a single flagpole in the center of the building, it should be used exclusively to hang the swastika party flag, and the black, white, and red national emblem should be hung in the center window. If there are two flagpoles side by side on the roof of the building, the swastika party flag should be hung to the right of the tricolor national flag. If there are three flagpoles, the tricolor national flag should be hung in the center, and the swastika party flags should be hung on both sides. The order also stated that this is a temporary measure, as the form of the national flag has not yet been decided and is being selected. (Guomin News Agency, 25th)

Gold and Silver: The price of gold in London continued to rise by 4.5 pence today (April 26th), quoted at 144 shillings and 9.5 pence. Judicial Yuan Interprets Doubts Regarding Accountants' Association 47

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan has recently interpreted the doubts regarding Article 16 of the Accountants Law as follows: Since Article 16, Paragraph 1 of the Accountants Law permits accountants to join an association in the nearest place and perform their duties, if an accountant, after joining an association in Place A, wants to perform duties in Place B, if Place B is the nearest place to Place A, even if an accountants' association is established in Place B at the same time or later, there is no reason to force them to join the association in Place B again. As to whether it is the nearest place, it should be determined based on the facts. (Central News Agency, 26th)

British-Russian Negotiations and the European Situation 78

— (European Correspondence)

Britain Temporarily Abandons Anti-Russian Policy; German-French Conflict May Thus Be Eased

After participating in the British-German negotiations in Berlin, the British Lord Privy Seal Eden then went to Moscow according to his scheduled itinerary. This is a large whale from the sea running to Eastern Europe to meet the giant bear on land, and it is happening at a time when the international situation is particularly urgent. Its significance is not only related to the future peace or war in Europe, but also whether the world can maintain the status quo depends on whether there is a possibility of compromise between the two sides in this negotiation.

The opposition between Britain and Russia has made international politics more complicated in recent years. For example, if Japan had forcibly seized the four eastern provinces of our country without Britain's tacit consent, then things would not have been so simple. If Germany had rearmed without Britain's secret protection, Hitler would not have dared to use such strong tactics. Naturally, Britain does not love Japan and Germany. Its consistent policy is nothing more than to plan to create an anti-Russian front. Therefore, after the Japanese army occupied Shenyang, the Japanese used the slogan of attacking Soviet Russia to fundamentally soften British public opinion. The Eastern Locarno Treaty was also forced to a dead end for French diplomats because Britain was unwilling to abandon its anti-Russian policy, allowing Germany to secretly expand its armaments at ease. Before the British-Russian negotiations were held, French newspapers were always worried that the incompatibility between Britain and Russia would make French diplomacy more difficult. In order to deal with Germany, France needs powerful military allies. In future wars, France cannot lack the land and air forces of Soviet Russia, and it also needs the help of the British navy. However, it is impossible to have both. France must choose one country, either allying with Britain or allying with Russia. Therefore, Laval felt it was difficult to please both sides. The difficulty in resolving the German-French issue in recent years is also due to the conflict between Britain and Russia.

Simon's visit to Berlin beforehand Germany held great hopes. Hitler had used the bold character of his Germanic soldiers and his special talent for speech, originally wanting to persuade Simon with the danger of communism and find a way out for Germany in the contradictions between Britain and Russia. However, it is simply wishful thinking to make a cold-blooded Englishman move emotionally and forget the interests of the British Empire. This is especially true of Foreign Minister Simon, who is proficient in law. People originally said that he was a "cold within cold" Englishman. This time, Hitler used German-style diplomacy and happened to meet him, so naturally it was not easy to gain any advantage.

In fact, although Britain's recent diplomatic route has aimed at opposing Russia, it has become clear since it was once greatly fooled by the Japanese that there are always better players. Others are not necessarily more stupid than the British, and they seem to be more careful than before. Because of its geographical distance from Soviet Russia and its historical feud with France, and although the National Socialist ideology conflicts with Soviet Russia, it is still questionable whether Germany can serve as the vanguard against Russia militarily. Britain sees this very clearly. What Simon wanted to understand in the British-German negotiations was not only to be satisfied with Germany's determination to oppose Russia, but also to see, first, whether an anti-Russian war could be realized, and second, whether Germany had other ambitions. Then he would decide on Britain's final attitude towards Germany. Hitler's answers to Simon on these two points still seemed to be a vague attitude. He treated the anti-Russian issue as the main subject of this negotiation, which was correct in principle, but he did not have any further proposals. This easily makes Britain feel that Germany is only using opposition to Soviet Russia as a slogan to coerce, and is actually pursuing other goals. For example, Hitler explained that Germany's rearmament was entirely due to defense against Russia. He vividly depicted Soviet Russia's plan to communize Europe and placed the responsibility of protecting culture on himself. This is Hitler's understanding of the British. In Simon's eyes, isn't National Socialist Germany and Communist Soviet Russia essentially the same? Everyone is a troublemaker. The most important thing is as long as it doesn't harm Britain's interests. Hitler believes that in addition to possessing millions of land troops, Soviet Russia also has the world's strongest air force. Moreover, when war breaks out, the major cities in eastern Germany are in danger of being bombed by the Soviet Russian air force. Therefore, Britain should sympathize with Germany's expansion of armaments. As for Germany's refusal to sign the Eastern Locarno Treaty, it is also for the same reason. Hitler believes that Germany and Soviet Russia have long had an irreconcilable attitude. If Germany joins a certain Eastern European security treaty, then once a certain anti-Soviet Russian country attacks Soviet Russia, it is simply impossible for Germany to send troops to help Soviet Russia. Similarly, when Germany is attacked by others, it cannot tolerate the Red Army entering German territory. In short, in order to ensure the security of Europe, Germany needs to be equal to Soviet Russia in terms of land and air forces. As for the navy, Germany demands at least equality with France, the purpose of which is said to be still to defend against Russia.

This time, Hitler may have misjudged the British. Although Britain hopes that Germany will be willing to be the vanguard against Russia, if it can really be realized, Britain may be willing to make more concessions. However, Hitler's chest-beating attitude has the aura of the Japanese. The matter has not yet been done, but he first wants a lot of benefits. This is what the British are unwilling to be fooled again. On the other hand, the monster of Germany is not only afraid of France, but also constantly wary of Britain. When Simon arrived in Berlin, it was just after Germany announced an increase in its military, and the whole country was in a state of war. In addition, Hitler himself personally told Simon that Germany's air force strength has caught up with Britain. Hitler's original intention may have been only to ingratiate himself with Britain, indicating that his strength is sufficient to serve as the vanguard against Russia. But in Simon's ears, the meaning is very different. Britain is afraid that Soviet Russia cannot be eliminated, and instead another Germany will emerge out of thin air, which is not good for the British Empire. As a result of the Berlin talks, because of the haggling between the two sides and their different goals, Britain and Germany were unable to reach a consensus on the point of anti-Russia. At this point, British politicians played their old tricks again, taking a step back and waiting for changes.

Just at this time, Eden ran to Moscow. The significance of these British-Russian negotiations for Soviet Russia is needless to say. Even Stalin - the uncrowned king of Soviet Russia today - never received foreign diplomats except for exchanges with the US ambassador to Russia. But this time was an exception. He met Eden. He asked whether Britain was allowing Germany to act freely in Eastern Europe. This is a very interesting contrast. The object of the talks in Moscow was Germany. Some people say that the only achievement of the British diplomat's visit to Germany and Russia this time is to make Germany and Russia openly curse each other. As for the entire European situation, it is still the same as before. What has changed may only be that Britain has temporarily abandoned its attempt to attack Soviet Russia.

If an anti-Russian war cannot be realized for a while, then there is a common ground between Britain and Russia: the hope for peace and the hope to find ways to maintain the status quo. This is especially true after Simon's visit to Berlin. On the one hand, Britain has understood Germany's true face, and on the other hand, the European situation does not allow Britain to have such a risky plan again. Therefore, British-Russian relations have taken a sharp turn for the worse.

The most important point of the Moscow talks this time is how to maintain peace in Europe. Soviet Russia's proposal is still to conclude an Eastern Locarno Treaty. Due to the provisions of this treaty, the eastern border of Soviet Russia is guaranteed by the strength of France and Czechoslovakia, and naturally it is no longer afraid of the actions of Germany and Poland. And Britain hopes for peace in Europe under the leadership of the League of Nations. After everyone's concessions, they accepted each other's proposals in principle. This means that Britain supports the signing of the Eastern Locarno Treaty, and Soviet Russia must also do its best to help the group convention under the leadership of Britain. What is the group convention? In other words, this is a variation of Britain's long-standing policy in Europe: maintaining the balance of power between countries. If this group convention is realized, then a balance of power will be created among the four European powers, France, Russia, Germany, and Italy. At that time, Britain's actions can influence the overall situation. We must not misunderstand London politicians and think that they will join the anti-German group after the failure of the British-German negotiations and force Hitler to surrender. On the contrary, Germany's resurgence will only make Britain's diplomacy more convenient. Therefore, in the future, whether Britain compromises with France and Russia or not, its long-standing pro-German attitude will probably not fundamentally change.

Britain's temporary abandonment of its anti-Russian policy seems to be purely for peace on the surface. London gentlemen are not only acting as mediators between Germany and Russia in Europe, but are even willing to consider the disputes between Japan and Russia in the Far East. For this "friendly" move by Britain, Soviet Russia must pay a material price. The most important condition for this exchange is that Soviet Russia must stop its communist propaganda in the British mainland and its territories. Only in this way will British politicians believe in Litvinov's theory of coexistence between socialist and capitalist countries. However, this condition is still not enough.

British trade with Russia in 1934 almost quadrupled compared to 1933, and the total value of exports to Russia in January of this year was £706,408, compared to only £548,482 in January of last year. In addition, Soviet Russia has announced to Britain that the cash that Russia used to transport to the United States every year will now be changed to London. In this way, Soviet Russia's orders in Britain will greatly increase. According to the opinions of Soviet Russian diplomats in Britain, if it is implemented according to the planned plan, the number of unemployed people in Britain can be reduced by 250,000 within three months. At a time when countries are suffering from unemployment problems, reducing 250,000 people is a huge temptation for Britain. Perhaps the economy is still the most important reason why Britain and Russia are moving towards compromise this time. Soviet Russia is good at using the weapon of foreign trade, and so British gentlemen also feel that they have to change their original attitude. This time, Moscow and Berlin are mutually pulling Britain, and because everyone's positions are different, their attitudes are also different. On the one hand, Germany is limited by the military character of the Germanic nation and cannot pretend to be "seemingly peaceful." On the other hand, Germany also needs to show some strength in order to gain Britain's trust and make the establishment of an anti-Russian front possible. Therefore, Germany can achieve its desired goals. So when Simon arrived in Berlin, Hitler sent his personal guards fully armed to the airfield to greet him. Soviet Russia is not like that. What Eden saw in Moscow this time was almost entirely about cultural construction, such as libraries, museums, dance in theaters, and the newly completed underground railway in Moscow. Even the Red Army club, which used to practice almost every day in the sky over the western suburbs of Moscow, did not see a single aircraft during the period when the British guests were in Moscow. Soviet Russia wanted to tell Britain that it only focuses on its domestic construction and has no intention of invading others. Originally, in international politics, everyone takes their own interests as the premise, so naturally there is no love or hate. The way Germany and Russia treat Simon and Eden is only a matter of form, and of course it will not affect Britain's fundamental attitude. But we must remember that Britain is still a country that is trying its best to avoid war, so this attitude of Soviet Russia will also have some effect on Britain.

We only need to compare the joint announcements of Britain and Germany and Britain and Russia to understand that Britain's attitude has been shaken. It is of course difficult to predict how the entire future European situation will change, but if the opposition between Britain and Russia is really eliminated, then Germany and France may be able to avoid a war. However, at this moment, it is not easy to rein in at the precipice. (April 3rd in Berlin)

Legislative Yuan Passes the Simple Life Insurance Law 79

The Legislative Yuan passed the Simple Life Insurance Law at its 14th meeting on the 26th. The original text is as follows: (Article 1) Simple life insurance is a state-owned enterprise and is under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Communications. Other insurance companies are not allowed to operate it. (Article 2) Simple life insurance is managed by the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau and directed by its branches or post offices.

Page 10

(Article 3) The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau is the insurer of simple life insurance and is responsible for paying the insured amount in accordance with this law. (Article 4) Simple life insurance is divided into two types: whole life insurance and term insurance. Whole life insurance pays the insured amount upon the death of the insured. Term insurance pays the insured amount when the contract expires or before it expires and the insured dies. (Article 5) The simple life insurance amount is limited to 50 to 500 national currency. If the same insured enters into several insurance contracts, the total amount of insurance shall not exceed 500 yuan. (Article 6) The revenue and expenditure of simple life insurance shall be based on national currency. (Article 7) Simple life insurance exempts the insured from physical examination. (Article 8) Insurance premium rates and accumulated amounts shall be determined by the articles of association. (Article 9) All citizens of the Republic of China who are at least twelve years old and no more than sixty years old may be insured. (Article 10) The policyholder shall pay the insurance premium in accordance with the articles of association. (Article 11) The policyholder may be the insured himself or another person. If another person is the insured, his consent shall be obtained in advance. The policyholder may designate or change the beneficiary before the occurrence of the claim event, but if the insured is another person, the consent of both shall be obtained. If no beneficiary is designated, in whole life insurance, the insured amount shall be regarded as the insured's estate. In term insurance, the insured shall be regarded as the beneficiary, and upon the death of the insured, the insured amount shall be regarded as the insured's estate. (Article 12) When another person is the insured, the policyholder or beneficiary must have a close economic interest with the insured in order to apply for the insurance. (Article 13) When applying for the insurance, the policyholder must truthfully pay or declare all matters that should be paid or declared as stipulated in the articles of association. (Article 14) After the insurer accepts the application, it shall carefully issue the insurance policy. The matters to be recorded on the insurance policy shall be determined by the articles of association. (Article 15) The insurance contract shall take effect from the date of issuance of the insurance policy. (Article 16) After the insurance contract takes effect, if the insured dies, the beneficiary shall enjoy benefits in accordance with the following provisions: (1) If the insured dies within six months, he shall receive all the insurance premiums that have been paid. (2) If the insured dies after six months but less than one year, he shall receive one-fifth of the insured amount. (3) If the insured dies after one year but less than two years, he shall receive half of the insured amount. (5) If the insured dies after two years, he shall receive the full insured amount. (Article 17) The policyholder may request to change the insurance contract in accordance with the articles of association. (Article 18) The policyholder may at any time declare to the insurer to terminate the contract, and the effect of the termination shall not be retroactive. (Article 19) If the policyholder fails to pay the insurance premium due within the period stipulated in the articles of association, the insurer shall suspend the effect of the contract. After the effect of the contract is suspended, the policyholder may change the contract to a single premium insurance contract within one month in accordance with the articles of association. (Article 20) If the effect of the insurance contract is suspended, the policyholder may apply for reinstatement within one year. When the insurer accepts the aforementioned application, it shall record the matter on the insurance policy and sign or affix a seal. The reinstatement of the insurance contract shall take effect from the date of signing or sealing. (Article 21) When the insurance contract is reinstated, it shall be deemed that its effect has never been suspended. (Article 22) After the insurance contract in the preceding article is reinstated, if the insured dies, the beneficiary shall enjoy benefits in accordance with the following provisions: If the insurance premium has been paid for more than two years when the insurance contract is suspended: (1) If the insured dies within six months, he shall receive the accumulated amount before reinstatement and the insurance premium paid after reinstatement. (2) If the insured dies after six months but less than one year, he shall receive the accumulated amount before reinstatement and half of the insured amount. (3) If the insured dies after one year, he shall receive the full insured amount. If the insurance premium has not been paid for more than one year when the insurance contract is suspended: (1) If the insured dies within one year, he shall receive the accumulated amount before reinstatement and the insurance premium paid after reinstatement. (2) If the insured dies after one year but less than two years, he shall receive the accumulated amount before reinstatement and half of the insured amount. (3) If the insured dies after two years, he shall receive the full insured amount. (Article 23) In any of the following circumstances, the insurer shall not be liable for compensation, except as provided in Article 24: (1) The insured commits suicide within one year after the insurance contract takes effect or is reinstated. (2) The policyholder intentionally causes the death of the insured. (3) The beneficiary intentionally causes the death of the insured, but if there are two or more beneficiaries, the benefits to which other beneficiaries are entitled shall not be affected. (4) The insured dies, and the policyholder or beneficiary fails to notify the insurer in accordance with the articles of association. (Article 24) In the event of any of the circumstances in Article 17, Article 18, Article 19, or Article 1 and Article 24, the beneficiary may request the return of a portion of the accumulated amount in accordance with the articles of association if the insurance premium has been paid for more than two years. (Article 25) If the insurance contract is established due to fraud by the policyholder, insured, or beneficiary, the insurer may rescind it. When the contract is rescinded in accordance with the provisions of the preceding paragraph, the policyholder shall not make any other requests except to request the return of a portion of the accumulated amount in accordance with the articles of association. (Article 26) The insurer of simple life insurance shall not subrogate the policyholder or beneficiary's right to claim against a third party arising from the insured event. (Article 27) The insurer of simple life insurance shall not request payment of the insurance premium through litigation. (Article 28) All rights arising from the insurance contract by the policyholder, insured, or beneficiary shall not be assigned or pledged to others except in accordance with the provisions of the articles of association. (Article 29) The rights arising from the insurance contract shall be extinguished if they are not exercised within five years from the date they can be claimed. (Article 30) If the insurance premium has been paid for more than two years, the policyholder may request a loan in accordance with the articles of association, but if the beneficiary is a third party, his consent shall be obtained. (Article 31) An incapacitated person or a person with limited capacity shall be deemed to have the capacity to act with respect to simple life insurance only with respect to the insurer. (Article 32) The accounting of simple life insurance shall be separated and independent from the accounting of other postal services. (Article 33) The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau shall announce the business and financial status of simple life insurance after the end of each fiscal year. (Article 34) The accumulated funds of simple life insurance shall not be used for other purposes except for investment methods as stipulated in the following clauses: (1) Loans to policyholders secured by insurance policies. (2) Purchasing government bonds issued by the central government, but the funds purchased shall not exceed 15% of the total accumulated funds and the total reserve funds. (3) Lending secured by reliable securities or warehouse receipts. (4) Lending secured by real estate with reliable income, but the total amount shall not exceed 15% of the total accumulated funds of the Bureau, and the mortgage amount shall not exceed 50% of the appraised value of the real estate. (5) Lending secured by the Bureau's fixed-term passbooks or deposit certificates. (6) Bill discounting. (7) Export financing. (8) Operating a warehousing business. (9) Agricultural lending. (10) Other lending for investment in state-owned production enterprises approved by the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau and the Supervisory Committee and approved by the Ministry of Communications, but the total amount shall not exceed 20% of the total accumulated funds. (Article 35) The business of simple life insurance shall be subject to the supervision of the Supervisory Committee of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau. (Article 36) Simple life insurance contracts and the benefits derived from the contracts, as well as all documents, vouchers, and registers, shall be exempt from all taxes. (Article 37) The supplementary rules and regulations to this law shall be drafted by the Ministry of Communications and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. (Article 38) The effective date and area of implementation of this law shall be determined by order separately.

Northwest Inspection Report 80

— Special Correspondent Ya of This Newspaper

The Thriving City of Xijing

Shaanxi was the ancient land of Yongzhou. The provincial capital is the old city of Xi'an Prefecture. The Zhou, Qin, Han, Western Wei, Northern Zhou, Sui, and Tang dynasties all established their capitals here or nearby. The Xi'an Prefecture governed Xianning and Chang'an counties. In the Republic of China, the prefectures and counties were abolished, and Xianning and Chang'an were merged, collectively known as Chang'an County. In the early Zhou Dynasty, the capital was Haojing, more than twenty li southwest of present-day Xi'an. When the capital was moved to Luoyang, Haojing was abandoned. Qin destroyed the six kingdoms and established its capital in Xianyang. Xianyang Palace was abandoned, and Epang Palace was built. Xiang Yu entered the pass and burned Epang Palace, and the Weiyang Palace of the Han Dynasty was completed. The Sui Dynasty built a new capital in present-day Chang'an, which was expanded in the early Tang Dynasty. The city was about eighteen li from east to west and fifteen li from north to south, with a circumference of sixty-seven li. Later, it was reduced in size again. In the early years of the Ming Dynasty, the old city of the Tang Dynasty was rebuilt. The Qing Dynasty followed suit, with only repairs. In the Republic of China, its old appearance was retained, and it was still named Xi'an. In the twenty-first year, the central government designated Luoyang as the acting capital and Xi'an as the auxiliary capital. The capital was Nanjing, and the acting capital was Tokyo, so Xi'an was known as Xijing, which originated in the Zhou Dynasty. It is also said that Xijing was the old name of the Han and Tang dynasties. The might of Emperor Wu of Han and Emperor Taizong of Tang shook the surrounding barbarians, which was the most glorious era of our Chinese nation. Now, renaming it Xijing is intended to learn from the past and encourage the future.

Today's Xi'an city is about seven li long from east to west and five li wide from north to south, with a circumference of nearly thirty li. The popular saying that it is ten li long and wide, with a circumference of forty li, is not true. The city wall is thirty-four feet high and three zhang thick at the top. The old gates were four: the east gate was called Changle, the west gate was called Anding, the south gate was called Yongning, and the north gate was called Anyuan. The east and west gates are slightly biased towards the south of the city, so the northern half of the city is larger than the southern half. When Feng Yuxiang's army was stationed in Shaanxi, two new gates were built in the northeast corner: the east-facing one was called Zhongshan Gate, and the north-facing one was called Zhongzheng Gate (formerly Yuxiang Gate, with the railway station outside). The old four gates each had a moat, a gate tower, and an arrow tower on the moat, reaching a height of ten zhang. Its grandeur can be compared with the city towers of Beiping. However, during the eight-and-a-half-month siege of the city by Liu Zhenhua in the fifteenth year, Yang Hucheng resisted and destroyed the wooden planks inside, which is a pity.

According to a survey in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, the population of Xijing city was 120,000. After the siege of the fifteenth year and the great drought of the seventeenth and eighteenth years, many people died, were injured, or fled. According to a survey in June of the twentieth year, there were only 108,000 people. Afterwards, it gradually increased year by year. According to the Construction Department, there were 114,389 people at the end of the twenty-first year, 121,583 people at the end of the twenty-second year, and 125,141 people at the end of last year. According to local people, the household registration of the urban area, if accurately investigated, should be at least 150,000 people or more. This spring, with the railway open, the population will increase sharply.

The commerce of Xijing city has shown a prosperous trend in recent years due to the increase in government agencies and the development of transportation. Areas such as Zhongshan Street (East Street), Zhubashi, and Minzhong Street (South Courtyard Gate) are all shops selling department stores, fine satin, leather goods, and paper. There are many new-style decorations. Hotels and restaurants, such as the Xijing Hotel and Northwest Hotel on Zhongshan Street, have rare architectural facilities in the Northwest. The streets are also very wide, with separate lanes for pedestrians and vehicles, which can avoid congestion. Newly planted pagoda trees and willows on both sides have greatly increased the beauty of the city. Qiaozikou on West Street has many grocery stores. Only the western half of North Street has many shops, while the eastern half does not. The area near the city is still all wasteland, showing a rather deformed development. South Street has mountain goods stores and jewelry shops. Other products from various places in southern Shaanxi, such as lacquer, hemp, and tung oil, are first sold in Nanguan. Transportation tools include cars, rickshaws, bicycles, horse-drawn carriages, large carts, and wheelbarrows. East and West Fire Streets, and from Zhongshan Gate to South Street, have started operating public buses this spring. The responsible authorities are gradually building macadam roads on various streets, but due to various reasons such as surveying levels, little attention has been paid to drainage ditches, so rainwater cannot be discharged, and sometimes it is very muddy. Various towns such as Caotan, Doumen, Xinzhu, Yinjiahui, and Duqu are also prosperous commercial areas belonging to the county. Glutinous rice crops are sold to Henan and Shanxi, and pig bristles and sheep wool are transported to Tianjin and Shanghai. The export of cotton has also increased year by year. Those transported in from outside are Hankou tea, Shanxi salt, Jiangzhe silk satin, Hubei copperware, and wheat flour from Bengbu and other places. The geology of Chang'an is loess, which is most suitable for agriculture. The Wei, Ba, Chan, Xiao, Feng, Zao, Jue, and Lao rivers all provide irrigation benefits. Secondly, well irrigation is used. Rich families use waterwheels, while poor people use manual labor to draw water, all of which can achieve their goals. Therefore, rice and hemp are grown in the fields, and every family has enough to eat. The terrain of the whole county is a rhomboid basin, slightly higher in the southeast and lower in the northwest. The areas of Xianyang and Sanyuan have become plateaus, and the west is surrounded by the Longban slopes, while the southeast is surrounded by the Qinling Mountains. Such fertile land and abundant rivers, with mountains and rivers as barriers, have been the reasons for choosing capitals here throughout the ages. The climate is hottest in summer, with temperatures reaching 90 to 100 degrees Fahrenheit. In winter, it drops to freezing point. Spring and autumn are in the 70s and 80s. Autumn is rainy, with overcast skies for ten days, almost like the plum rains in Jiangnan. Spring needs rain the most, but rainfall is lacking, hence the saying "spring rain is as precious as oil." If there is an east wind in spring and a west wind after autumn, it can bring rain. There is also the saying "Chang'an has always had west wind and rain." There is snow in winter and early spring. When the north wind arrives, everything is frozen solid, and water drips into ice. Well water is very scarce. Only the Sweet Water Well near the West Gate in the city, the Saintly Woman Spring in the northwest suburbs of the city, and the Double Dragon Pool west of the Niutou Temple in the south of the city are the three famous springs of Chang'an. Shaanxi Province is the birthplace of ancient Chinese culture, and Chang'an was the capital of the Zhou, Qin, Han, and Tang dynasties. There are too many famous scenic spots and historical sites to see: (1) The Chang'an Mountains, branched from the Qinling Mountains, form peaks everywhere, with different names in different places, such as Qinghua Mountain, Guanyin Mountain, Xiaowutai, and Cuihua Mountain, but Nanwutai is the most secluded and beautiful. The car road is open, and many contemporary talents visit it. (2) The First Provincial Library is where Zhang Zai, Cheng Yi, and Cheng Hao lectured in the cave dwellings. It has been rebuilt. In addition to books, it also houses the Zhou Ding, Qin and Han ancient artifacts, the Tang Bell, and the Zhaoling stone carvings of horses. (Note: These stones were carved when Emperor Taizong of Tang buried Empress Wende. Originally there were six horses, but in the fifth year of the Republic of China, they were stolen and sold to foreigners by powerful people, smashed and driven away. The people of Shaanxi recovered four of them.) and other antiques, more than two hundred and seventy pieces large and small. (3) The Stele Forest is located in the Dongfu School in the South Gate, which is the old site of the Tang Imperial College. Many steles of various calligraphers such as Yan, Liu, Chu, and Ou are stored inside, hence the name Stele Forest. There are a total of 472 kinds of steles, with more than 2,400 stones of various sizes. (4) The Bell Tower was built in the west corner of the city in the seventeenth year of Hongwu in the Ming Dynasty. In the tenth year of Wanli, it was moved to the center of the city. It has three floors and is more than ten zhang high. It used to house an astronomical museum and a public lecture hall. Now it is stationed by the army. The Drum Tower in front of the southeast provincial government has nine bays and four floors, about eighty-six feet high. Walking up the eaves steps, it is sixty-eight steps long from east to west and thirty-eight steps wide from north to south. Climbing high and looking out, the whole city is in sight, giving a sense of "a dangerous building is a thousand feet high, and you can pick the stars and clouds by hand." (5) The Big Wild Goose Pagoda is in the Ci'en Temple eight li southeast of the city. It has seven floors. The base of the pagoda is fourteen zhang on each side and about eighteen zhang high. There is a spiral staircase to climb to the top. There are many steles with inscriptions from past dynasties in front of it, which is what is called the inscription of the Wild Goose Pagoda. (6) Jianfu Temple was the old residence of Emperor Yang of Sui when he lived in the vassal state. Later, it was donated as a temple. There is a tall pagoda in it, with fifteen floors, facing the Big Wild Goose Pagoda, so it is called the Small Wild Goose Pagoda. During the earthquake in the Jiajing period of the Ming Dynasty, the pagoda split into two. Later, another earthquake slightly reunited the crack, about a foot wide, forming a straight line from top to bottom, which is truly a spectacle. (7) Yangta Temple is said to be the Sui Baoqing Temple or built by the sisters of Yang Guifei in the Tang Dynasty. (8) The Temple of Literature has magnificent halls and towering ancient cypresses, built since the Zhenguan period of the Tang Dynasty. (9) Lotus Lake Park, Songjia Garden, Qingzhen Temple Niutou Temple, Du Fu Temple, Dong Zhongshu Temple, Qujiang Pool, and other places are all scenic spots for sightseeing. The Xijing Preparatory Committee and the Xijing Municipal Construction Committee are not only planning and building the city, but also striving to preserve historical sites, seeking to restore the beauty of Zhongnan and Shanglin, and tracing the prosperity of the Zhou, Qin, Han, and Tang dynasties, which is not only for attracting tourists and prospering the market.

Cai Tingkai Returns to China; To Recuperate in Hong Kong for a Short Period; The Trip to Guilin Province is Not True 81

Guangzhou dispatch: Cai Tingkai, the former commander-in-chief of the 19th Route Army, arrived in Hong Kong on the Coolidge wheel via the Philippines at six o'clock in the morning on the 19th of this month. Comrades and old subordinates who welcomed him at the Hong Kong pier beforehand included Chen Mingshu, Shen Guanghan, Tan Qixiu, Qiu Zhaochen, Deng Shizeng, Weng Guiqing, Ye Shaoquan, and Cai's younger brother Chao Kai, and others, more than ten people in all. Although Mr. Cai showed a slightly weary look when he disembarked, he was in better spirits than before. After shaking hands and exchanging greetings with those who welcomed him, he returned to his private residence on Shancun Road, Happy Valley. According to Mr. Cai's remarks to visitors, he left for overseas on April 11th last year and arrived in Italy on May 5th. He then successively inspected various countries in mainland Europe, and then went to England. Due to the urgency of the question of time in all the places he went, he just took a cursory look, and failed to conduct a deep investigation. From the surface observation, various European countries are now implementing control over the economy, and there is a phenomenon of the rise of heavy industry. The military preparations of various countries are all being greatly improved and expanded. At present, Germany is the center of the European issue. Since the signing of a secret agreement between Japan, Germany, and Poland, Japan has used Germany to contain the European powers in order to fulfill its ambition to develop arbitrarily in East Asia. Italy has recently been striving to rectify its military preparations. The fascist organization is tightly knit, and the rulers are truly able to be selfless and sincere for the country. The German people are disciplined and orderly, France has a bright culture, and the people love the country. The people of Belgium and Switzerland work hard in industry and fully demonstrate the spirit of autonomy. British society is stable and the people abide by the law. All of these can be models for our country from top to bottom. The United States has recently experienced overproduction and a sharp increase in unemployment, and its finances still need to be reorganized. Overseas Chinese in our country suffer all kinds of unequal treatment and are greatly affected by the recession, experiencing great pain. The present return to the country will be to rest in Hong Kong, and it is not intended to go elsewhere in the short term. The rumors that I am going to Guilin Province are not true. (20th)

Jiangxi Province: The Tragic Decline of the Timber Industry; Exports Drop from Over Eight Million to Just Over One Million 82

Nanchang dispatch: Jiangxi Province has a mild climate and fertile land, which is very suitable for the reproduction of forests. In particular, cedar and camphor wood are the most abundant and famous products. Cedar wood is everywhere, and there is a lack of statistics on production. What can be used as a reference is the tax levied by the tax bureau. According to the survey and statistics on timber specialties conducted by the Jiangxi Special Commissioner of the Ministry of Finance in the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, the old Ganzhou Prefecture produced 5 to 6 million branches annually, the counties near Ji'an produced about 6 to 7 million branches, Jianchang produced about 2 million branches, Fuzhou produced about 1 million branches, Xiushui River basin produced about 2 million branches, Fuliang produced more than 100,000 branches, and Wuyuan Dexing produced more than 100,000 branches, Guangfeng and other counties produced more than 200,000 branches, totaling 16 to 17 million branches. According to the calculation of two codes at the same time, the annual output is more than 350,000 taels of two codes, with a total value of more than 5.83 million yuan. This kind of number is just an estimate, but analyzing the timber sold in Changzhou for 10 million yuan, the annual value of Jiangxi Province is about 7 million yuan to 8 million yuan. In the past, the timber produced in Jiangxi Province was collected in Wucheng by the Gan River, Fu River, and Xiu River, and transported to Nanjing and the Yangtze River area. In society, timber merchants and salt merchants were known side by side as great merchants. However, in recent years, the situation has been very different. The number of sales has plummeted. Most timber merchants have no foothold. The tax bills issued by the Jiangxi Production and Sales Tax Bureau from June 21st to May 22nd of the Republic of China, in one year, the timber transported out of the province was 1,400,000,1609 branches, and the average value was calculated at one yuan, for a total of 1.4 million yuan, which is only one-eighth of the peak period. The tragedy of the decline is truly alarming. The biggest reasons are: (1) Natural disasters and man-made disasters, important production areas have fallen into the hands of bandits for eight years, production has been cut off, and goods have been abandoned on the ground, even if there are a few, they cannot be transported out. (2) Foreign loans and foreign timber are selling well. The import of foreign timber has increased more than ten times in twenty years. In the twentieth year of the Republic of China, the value of timber imports reached 3,168,4806 yuan. (3) Adhering to the old methods and not knowing how to add artificial sawing and planing to compete with foreign pine that saves labor and materials will eventually lead to failure. (April 22nd)

Wuxi: Football Star Drowns After Boat Capsizes 83

Qian Shiyi, a football star from Shanghai Nanguang, was 26 years old and a native of Ganlu Town in this county. A few days ago, Qian returned to Wuxi from Shanghai at the invitation of his friend Yang Fuyuan to watch the incense gathering at Furong Mountain in the northern countryside. Yesterday, Qian and three or four friends rowed a small boat from the mountain village to the city, leisurely wandering in the heart of the river, advancing slowly. At about 2 p.m., when sailing near Changxin Bridge on Guangqin Road, a Xiangyu steamboat suddenly came from behind at full speed, surging waves, and the momentum was very strong. The small boat Qian and others were driving was agitated by the huge waves, causing it to capsize. Qian and the other four people fell into the river at the same time. The river surface was wide and Qian, who did not know how to swim, was tragically submerged. The other three people swam to the shore and climbed up. They reported to the map head Tang Rengen, who reported to the court for an autopsy. The Xiangyu steamboat that caused the accident had already escaped.

Beijing-Wuxi-Wujin Silk Industry Joint Petition 84

During the Qing Guangxu period (16th and 17th years), silk and satin merchants in Wuxi, together with colleagues in Nanjing, Wujin, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hankou, organized the Jiangsu-Yu-Ning Guild Halls in Hangzhou to provide accommodation for the industry and to directly handle goods with silk weaving households. At that time, it was presented to the Zhejiang Governor and the county government for approval and filing. It has been more than 30 years. Recently, the silk industry has declined. The merchants in Anhui, Jiangxi, Hankou, and other places no longer go directly to Hangzhou to handle goods. Only the merchants in Beijing, Wujin and Wuxi still go to Hangzhou to purchase goods directly from the weaving households in the guild hall. However, last year, the Hangzhou Municipal Silk Industry Market planned to formulate methods for registering and receiving goods on behalf of customers in the guild hall. All those who previously purchased goods from the weaving households in the guild hall must enter the market. After registration, they must pay a deposit of 500 yuan, and also pay market service fees and equipment fees. The payment for the goods received must also be handed over to the market, and the weaving households will be given a long-term check separately. It has been approved and announced by Zhou Xiangxian, the mayor of Hangzhou. The silk industry in Beijing and Wuxi believes that business is absolutely free according to law. The silk industry market should not be restricted suddenly. Moreover, the industry has always paid in cash for goods, but now it is suddenly changed to promissory notes, which is obviously exploiting the weaving households, and the layer-by-layer extraction is even worse than the exchange. In addition to separately sending letters to the chambers of commerce in various places requesting the Hangzhou Municipal Government to revoke the registration and receipt methods, the colleagues in Nanjing and Wujin also elected representatives Jin Huanwen and others to come to Wuxi and unite with the colleagues in Wuxi to hold a meeting in the Wuxi Silk and Cloth Industry Guild Hall to agree that the colleagues in Beijing, Wuxi, and Wujin will immediately petition the Ministry of Industry of the Executive Yuan to cancel the methods in order to benefit the merchants.

Changzhou: Bandit Xu Renkun Executed by Shooting 85

Chen Bojiu, the captain of the third squadron of the Wuyi Security Corps, received a secret report on the 6th of last month that Xu Renkun of Qianhengtang, near Shishe, had partnered to rob the family of Tan Sheng, a villager, and burned the victims to death. He immediately led the team in disguise to arrest him. After detailed interrogation by the team, he confessed without denial. He was then sent to the county government for interrogation. After repeated summons to the victims to verify the evidence, he was sentenced to death. He was presented to the provincial government for review. Yesterday (25th), he was ordered to be executed by shooting. County magistrate Hou sent a team to sign and bring the prisoner to the case, verified his identity, and tied him to the Fenweidun execution ground for execution by shooting at 3 p.m.

Zhenjiang: Debt Collection Turns Violent in a Tragic Incident 86

In Yaojiaqiao, the fifth district of Dongxiang County, there is a resident named Zhao Yunlong, 34 years old, who works as a partner in a certain iron shop in the town. Last year, he borrowed ten yuan from his colleague Nie Changde, but he could not get it back after repeated requests. The other day, he went to Nie to recover the debt. They disagreed and started fighting each other. Both of them were holding iron hammers, and they fought fiercely for a long time. Unexpectedly, Zhao accidentally hit Nie's head with a hammer, and his brain was splashed out. He immediately fell to the ground and died. When the neighbors saw the murder, they arrested Zhao and sent him to the Fifth District Office, and then transferred him to the court for nailing and custody.

Four robberies occurred in Huang Qiao, the ninth district of the county, at 6 p.m. the day before yesterday. It is reported that those who were robbed that day were Zeng Wenda, a farmer in Lujiazui, and Zhang Dafa, Li Tianbao, and Li Sanbao, all fishermen. In addition to being robbed of property and clothing, Li Erbao was also robbed of ten thousand copper coins. Zeng Wenda and Li Sanbao were each robbed of a small boat. The people in the area have been quite alarmed since the robberies occurred.

The Dai surname cake shop in Sian Town abused Sun Zhao, a 17-year-old apprentice, at night, using an iron hammer and pen, abandoning the body in the toilet, and hanging it with a rope, making it look like a suicide.
